 Know about Babur (1) Babur ruled from 1526 AD to 1530 AD
 (2)24 farvari, 1483 i
 'zaheeruddin Muhammad Babur' was born in Farragna
 (3)babar apane pita kii ore se taimur kaa paanchavaa evam mata kii ore se changez khan kaa chaudaavaan vanshaj tha
 (4) Babur's father Umar Sheikh Mirza was the ruler of a small kingdom named Fargana
 (5)babar fergana kii gaddi par 8 june 1494 i main baitha
 (6) Babur assumed the title of Emperor in 1507 AD, which was not held by any Timur ruler till now
 (7)babar kii maatrubhaasha chaghtai bhashaa thi lekin farsi main babar ko maharath hasil thi
 He wrote his biography in Babri Nama in Chagatai
 (8)1526 i
 The Mughal dynasty was established in India with the defeat of Sultan Ibrahim Lodi of the last dynasty (lodi dynasty) of the Delhi Sultanate in the First War of Panipat
 (9)is vansh kaa sansthaapak "zahiruddin mohammad babar" tha

 (10)babar ne bharat par paanch baar akraman kiya

 (12)babar dwaara lade gaye pramukh yuddh the:(i)panipat kaa pratham yuddh 21 april, 1526 i
 Ko took place between Ibrahim Lodi and Babur, in which Babur won
 (ii)khanavaa kaa yuddh 17 march 1527 i main rana sanga or babar ke bich hua, jisamen babar kii jeet hui
 (iii) The war of Chanderi took place between Medni Rai and Babur on 29 March 1528 AD, in which Babur won
 (iv)ghaghara kaa yuddh 6 may 1529 i main afgano or babar ke bich hua, jisamen babar kii jeet hui
 (13) Babur used the Tugallama warfare policy for the first time in the First War of Panipat
 (14)ustad ali or mustafa babar ke do nishanebaaj the, jisane panipat ke pratham yuddh main bhaag liya tha

 Neem has been used for centuries to treat many diseases
 medical science main bhi neem kaa istemaal kai dawaaiyon ko banane main kiya jaataa he
 Neem has many such properties, which not only prove beneficial for health, but also greatly benefit the skin
 neem khun ko bhi saaf karata he
 Let's know about the countless benefits of chewing neem leaves
 
 
 1
 Beneficial for the skin - Neem leaves have anti-bacterial properties
 ye skin infections, munhasein or kai prakaan kii skin sambandhi samasyaon se raahat dilaataa he
 Applying paste of neem leaves with turmeric on skin problems like insect bites, itching, ringworm etc
 is beneficial
 neem chehre ke dane auradhabbebhi dur karata he
 2
 baalo ke liye phydemand-neem ke pattey chabane se baalo ko bhi phayda pahunchataa he
 Neem protects the scalp from damage from free radicals
 neem main maujuud anti-fungal gun sedandrofaki samasya dur hoti he
 For this, boiling neem leaves in water, washing hair with that water not only removes dandruff, as well as relieves other hair problems
 3
 Strengthening the immune system - Neem has antioxidant as well as antimicrobial, antiviral properties
 neem ke pattey chabane se immune system majboot banataa he
 Actually, chewing neem destroys the bacteria present in the body, which keeps the body safe from many diseases
 4
 Improves Digestion - Neem is also very beneficial for the liver, which naturally improves digestion

 As a result, along with the walls and roofs of those houses, cracks and large pits formed in the ground
 chhaton se pankhe or malbe ke girane ke baad logon ko pataa chalaa ki unke gharon ke neeche se pipeline nikali ja rahi he

 tippaniyan The finance ministry said in a statement that under the simplified arrangement, states would be given one-time consent to take loans based on their borrowing calendar for the first nine months of the current financial year

 Till now, each state was required to get approval from the Central Government on quarterly basis for market borrowings under the net lending limit as per the formula laid down by the 14th Finance Commission

 manthali active yugers 1 arab se bhi zyada hai
 Keeping in mind the increasing cyber fraud and phishing, you should be careful while using this app
 whatsap and tu and ancripshan detaa he
 Under which the message can be decoded by no third except the sender and receiver
 kai baar havers whatsap kaa sahaara lekar yugers takakhataranaak mailaware bhejte hanore use clic karne ko kaha jaataa he
 In such a situation, the risk of hacking your smartphone increases
 whatsap ke mutabik yugers ko yah ap yuj karte samay ye saavdhaanee baratani chahie
 The company has given some methods of safety which you can use according to your convenience
 - kisi bhi aise massej ko forverd karne se bachein jis par aapako thodaa bhi andeh ho
 You can block the sender sending such messages and delete that message
 - kisi bhi massej ko forverd karte samay saavdhaanee baraten- apni contact list kii jaanch karen or sirf un logon ko hi inamen rakhen jin par aap bharosa karte hai
 Also, do not join unknown groups
 in baton kaa bhi rakhen dhyankisi bhi aise massej main jise aadhikarik bataaya ja rahaa he usamen ssailing or grammer check kar len
 In any message, if whatsapp is asking for money from you for subscription, then it is wrong
 kyonki whatsap yuj karne ke liye koi paise nahin dene hote hai
 Ignore the message in which you are asked to click on it or share or install it to activate a new feature
 kisi bhi aise massej par clic bhul kar na karen jisamen aapse bank acount kii jaankaree yaa lotry ke paise milane kii baat ho
 You can block the sender that sends such messages continuously
 aise massej ko delit kar den
 It would be better to report such messages on whatsapp
 iske liye whatsap main hi opshan hota he yaa computer se whatsap web ke jariye bhi aap report kar sakate hai
 To report, you can click on About and Help in the settings option provided in the menu of whatsapp in Android Smartphone
